	<script type='text/javascript'>
		window.Adomik = window.Adomik || {};
		Adomik.randomAdGroup = function() {
			var rand = Math.random();
			switch (false) {
				case !(rand < 0.09):
					return "ad_ex" + (Math.floor(100 * rand));
				case !(rand < 0.10):
					return "ad_bc";
				default:
					return "ad_opt";
			}
		};
	</script>
